9th to 32nd Decklists of Grand Prix Prague 2018
===============================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on August 26, 2018 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/henke_author.jpg)
By Tobi Henke











The pilots of the following decks didn't make it to the playoffs, but they came pretty close. Yuya Hosokawa, Timo Seegelken, and Leszek Luty even managed to reach the same point totals during the Swiss rounds as six of the Top 8 players …







#### Yuya Hosokawa's Company, 9th


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
